---
## 🌀 Related Collections

```dataviewjs
const current = dv.current();
let currentTopics = [];
let currentAuthors = [];

if (current && current.topics) {
  currentTopics = Array.isArray(current.topics) ? current.topics : [current.topics];
}
if (current && current.authors) {
  currentAuthors = Array.isArray(current.authors) ? current.authors : [current.authors];
}

if (currentTopics.length === 0 && currentAuthors.length === 0) {
  dv.paragraph("No topics or authors specified in this note.");
} else {
  let related = dv.pages()
    .where(p => p.file.name !== current.file.name)
    .where(p =>
      (Array.isArray(p.topics) && p.topics.some(t => currentTopics.includes(t))) ||
      (Array.isArray(p.authors) && p.authors.some(a => currentAuthors.includes(a)))
    );

  let seen = new Set();
  let uniqueRelated = [];
  for (let p of related) {
    if (!seen.has(p.file.name)) {
      seen.add(p.file.name);
      uniqueRelated.push(p);
    }
  }

  if (uniqueRelated.length === 0) {
    dv.paragraph("No related notes found.");
  } else {
    dv.list(
      uniqueRelated.map(p => {
        // Compose author string if authors exist
        let authorString = (p.authors && p.authors.length)
          ? ` (${Array.isArray(p.authors) ? p.authors.join(", ") : p.authors})`
          : "";
        return `${dv.fileLink(p.file.name)}${authorString}`;
      })
    );
  }
}
```
